vsop87_data.c
Go to the documentation of this file.
1 /* data tables for planetary solution VSOP87
2  *
3  * created by automatic conversion from original distribution files at
4  * ftp://ftp.bdl.fr/pub/ephem/planets/vsop87/
5  *
6  * Each coordinate is calculated as:
7  *
8  * x = Sum{ T^alpha * A * cos( B + C*T ) }
9  *
10  * x is the coordinate in rad or a.u.
11  * T is the VSOP time in Julian Millenia(!) since J2000.0
12  * Note: the time argument in VSOP87 theory is equal to TAI + 32.184 s
13  *
14  * A (scaled by VSOP_ASCALE), B, C given below for each x and alpha
15  * run-of-the mill for each planet in one array vx_planet[][3].
16  * The block-boundary indices for each spatial dimension are then listed
17  * in a separate array vn_planet[][3].
18  *
19  * Truncation errors given in comments are from the authors' empirical
20  * formula: 2*sqrt(number of retained terms)*A[last retained]
21  */
22 
23 /* version d4 (lbr)
24  * heliocentric dynamical ecliptic and equinox of the date
25  */
26
